## [Attila Adorjany](http://www.comicvine.com/attila-adorjany/26-58724/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/5/59026/1108891-attila_image_3_icon.jpg" align="right" />##

Other comic contributions include Victory, Planet of the Apes, Beowulf, The Night driver, Warhammer, Popgun.

## [Jerry Robinson](http://www.comicvine.com/jerry-robinson/26-9680/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/6/69676/1598376-jerry_robinson_icon.jpg" align="right" />##
Legendary artist & creator rights advocate involved in the creation of Robin and the Joker.  In 2004, he was inducted to the Comic Book Hall of Fame.  Jerry Robinson was the president and is the founder of the Cartoonists and Writers Syndicate/Cartoon Arts International.

## [Roy Thomas](http://www.comicvine.com/roy-thomas/26-42067/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/229/102925-57421-roy-thomas_icon.jpg" align="right" />##
Roy Thomas is a longtime comic book writer and editor. Thomas started his career at Marvel Comics as a writer and later editor, he has written comics for Archie, Charlton, DC, Heroic Publishing, Marvel, Topps over the years. Thomas currently edits the fanzine Alter Ego.

## [Ryan Winn](http://www.comicvine.com/ryan-winn/26-43265/) <img src="http://media.comicvine.com/uploads/0/229/399512-40447-ryan-winn_icon.jpg" align="right" />##
Ryan Winn is a freelance artist most known for his comic book inking. Aside from inking tons of Marvel stuff he is most know for his inks on Spawn, The Darkness, and WildCATs.

He was nominated for best inker in 2009 for both the Harvey Award and The Comic Horro Award.
